This is a hotel that you can choose directly when you come to Hangzhou without hesitation!

msg:In one sentence: Zhongke Jiutai Hotel is a good hotel that is delayed by its name. It is highly recommended. The day before check-in, the housekeeper Tina called to inquire about the arrival time in order to prepare the room. After arriving at the store, I found that the room was indeed ready and arranged a high floor as required. Thanks to Tina. I originally booked a deluxe room, but after arriving in the room, I felt that I wanted to experience the river view room more, so after discussing with the front desk, I paid (not much) to upgrade to the river view room on the 17th floor. The river view room really has a much better view and a larger area. It is facing the big lotus, the CBD park is downstairs, and the city balcony is not far away. The new Chinese design of the hotel is great, especially the lobby, which is very beautiful. The design of the room also reveals a strong Chinese style everywhere, which is elegant and a**ospheric. There is a golden birdcage decoration at the door of each room, and the shapes are different, which leaves a deep impression before entering the room. The high-rise rooms facing the Qiantang River are spacious and bright, equipped with independent cloakrooms, toilets and bathrooms. Electric curtains, Kohler smart toilets, Dyson hair dryers, etc. are needless to say. The shower room is also equipped with massage nozzles, which makes it very comfortable to take a bath. The hotel's gym and swimming pool are open until 23:00. Although it is on the B1 floor, the light is bright and the swimming pool has a whole wall of green plants, which does not make people feel depressed. The water temperature of the swimming pool is moderate, and there is also a warm water massage pool next to it. It is very refreshing to take a dip in the hotel after a day of playing outside. In addition, there is a small and exquisite sky garden on the top floor of the hotel on the 18th floor. You can enter with the room card. The view of the scenery on both sides of the Qiantang River in the garden is particularly good. It is worth mentioning that the hotel's breakfast, although not many varieties, is of good quality. Blueberries, raspberries, strawberries and kiwis are all available in unlimited quantities. I also tried the special Wenzhou glutinous rice for the first time, which is also delicious. In addition, there are waffles and black truffle scrambled eggs on order, which are much better than the breakfast of the Xizi Hotel where I stayed before. All the staff in the entire hotel, from the front desk, concierge to the housekeeping depar**ent, are well-trained. Everyone is gentle and polite. No matter where they meet, they will take the initiative to say hello. The aunt who cleans the room will help fold the clothes that are randomly placed, roll up the charging cable and store it neatly. The doorman will take the initiative to open the door every time and help carry the luggage. In short, the experience of staying at Zhongke Jiutai Hotel was very good. The room rate of more than 1,000 during the 5.1 period can be said to be very cost-effective. I will definitely choose to stay here again when I come to Hangzhou in the future. However, from my observation, although it was 5.1, the occupancy rate of the entire hotel was not particularly high. I don‚Äôt know if it has anything to do with the hotel‚Äôs name change from Diaoyutai to Zhongke Jiutai. I hope the hotel‚Äôs business will get better and better.

I took a taxi to the hotel. The doorman did not take the initiative to open the door. He didn‚Äôt care and I never cared. After entering the hotel, I quickly found the front desk. A lady at the hotel found me and asked me if I would check in. She took me to the front desk. The front desk check-in was a butler-style check-in, so I didn‚Äôt have to stand. There were two places to check in. The lady at the front desk was doing something with the manager and would not accept me. The other place was checking in. After the queue ended and it was my turn, the lady at the front desk took my ID card. Then there was a silence for several minutes. After a long time, the words that broke the silence were, "Sir, the rooms you booked on the high floors are all gone. There is only one room on the 7th floor." After I confirmed the room type with her, it was an open-style river view suite. It was impossible to upgrade my room because I arrived too late (18:00). Then they gave me another excuse. A team came and booked all the rooms except this one. OK, 7th floor is 7th floor. After signing to confirm and swiping the pre-authorization, I was not shown to the room or the elevator. They just said that the elevator is on the right hand side behind you. In this case, I suggest that the hotel should not have the butler-style check-in, remove the chairs, and it is more reasonable to check in while standing. After entering the elevator, there was no 7th floor to go to. I thought I had gone to the wrong place. After asking other staff, I learned that the 7th floor is an apartment, not a hotel room. I have to go to another building and another elevator. What about my open-plan river view suite? I went back to the front desk and was greeted by another receptionist. It seemed that she was done with her work. The original receptionist didn‚Äôt even look at me and didn‚Äôt apologize at all. After I explained my purpose, the lady said that she would help me move to a hotel room on the 10th floor. I asked why she gave me an apartment before. The lady explained that the two rooms were very similar. They had put away all the cooking utensils in the apartment room. She also explained to me why the apartment room had cooking utensils. I was really amused. So your hotel has always sold apartment rooms as hotel rooms? Then at this time, the original receptionist didn‚Äôt even look at us and said that the room on the 10th floor was occupied. Are the rooms really so scarce? I stayed there until 11pm and felt a little hungry. I wanted to order food from my room, but I didn‚Äôt find the menu for ordering food from my room.
